Problem: add-two-numbers?list=neetcode250

<!DOCTYPE html><html lang="en" class="dark-theme"><head>
    <meta charset="utf-8">
    <title>Add Two Numbers - NeetCode</title>
    <meta name="description" content="Leetcode 2. Add Two Numbers

You are given two **non-empty** linked lists, `l1` and `l2`, where each represents a non-negative integer.
    
The digits are stored in **reverse order**, e.g. the number 123 is represented as `3 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 1 -&gt;` in the linked list.

Each of the nodes contains a single digit. You may assume the two numbers do not contain any leading zero, except the number 0 itself.

Return the sum of the two numbers as a linked list.

**Example 1:**

![](https://imagedelivery.net/CLfkmk9Wzy8_9HRyug4EVA/fee72e19-6a21-45a5-365e-3cb45aba9700/public)

```java
Input: l1 = [1,2,3], l2 = [4,5,6]

Output: [5,7,9]

Explanation: 321 + 654 = 975.
```

**Example 2:**

```java
Input: l1 = [9], l2 = [9]

Output: [8,1]
```

**Constraints:**
* `1 &lt;= l1.length, l2.length &lt;= 100`.
* `0 &lt;= Node.val &lt;= 9`

&lt;br&gt;
&lt;br&gt;
&lt;details class=&quot;hint-accordion&quot;&gt;  
    &lt;summary&gt;Recommended Time &amp; Space Complexity&lt;/summary&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
    You should aim for a solution with &lt;code&gt;O(m + n)&lt;/code&gt; time and &lt;code&gt;O(1)&lt;/code&gt; space, where &lt;code&gt;m&lt;/code&gt; is the length of list &lt;code&gt;l1&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;n&lt;/code&gt; is the length of list &lt;code&gt;l2&lt;/code&gt;.
    &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;

&lt;br&gt;
&lt;details class=&quot;hint-accordion&quot;&gt;  
    &lt;summary&gt;Hint 1&lt;/summary&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
    Try to visualize the addition of two numbers. We know that the addition of two numbers is done by starting at the one's digit. We add the numbers by going through digit by digit. We track the extra value as a &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt; because the addition of two digits can result in a number with two digits. The &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt; is then added to the next digits, and so on. How do you implement this in case of linked lists?
    &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;

&lt;br&gt;
&lt;details class=&quot;hint-accordion&quot;&gt;  
    &lt;summary&gt;Hint 2&lt;/summary&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
    We track the extra value, &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt;, here as well. We iterate through the lists &lt;code&gt;l1&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;l2&lt;/code&gt; until both lists reach &lt;code&gt;null&lt;/code&gt;. We add the values of both nodes as well as the carry. If either of the nodes is &lt;code&gt;null&lt;/code&gt;, we add &lt;code&gt;0&lt;/code&gt; in its place and continue the process while tracking the carry simultaneously. Once we complete the process, if we are left with any &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt;, we add an extra node with that carry value and return the head of the result list.
    &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;
">

.monaco-progress-container {
	width: 100%;
	height: 5px;
	overflow: hidden; /* keep progress bit in bounds */
}

.monaco-progress-container .progress-bit {
	width: 2%;
	height: 5px;
	position: absolute;
	left: 0;
	display: none;
}

.monaco-progress-container.active .progress-bit {
	display: inherit;
}

.monaco-progress-container.discrete .progress-bit {
	left: 0;
	transition: width 100ms linear;
}

.monaco-progress-container.discrete.done .progress-bit {
	width: 100%;
}

.monaco-progress-container.infinite .progress-bit {
	animation-name: progress;
	animation-duration: 4s;
	animation-iteration-count: infinite;
	transform: translate3d(0px, 0px, 0px);
	animation-timing-function: linear;
}

.monaco-progress-container.infinite.infinite-long-running .progress-bit {
	/*
		The more smooth `linear` timing function can cause
		higher GPU consumption as indicated in
		https://github.com/microsoft/vscode/issues/97900 &
		https://github.com/microsoft/vscode/issues/138396
	*/
	animation-timing-function: steps(100);
}

/**
 * The progress bit has a width: 2% (1/50) of the parent container. The animation moves it from 0% to 100% of
 * that container. Since translateX is relative to the progress bit size, we have to multiple it with
 * its relative size to the parent container:
 * parent width: 5000%
 *    bit width: 100%
 * translateX should be as follow:
 *  50%: 5000% * 50% - 50% (set to center) = 2450%
 * 100%: 5000% * 100% - 100% (do not overflow) = 4900%
 */
@keyframes progress { from { transform: translateX(0%) scaleX(1) } 50% { transform: translateX(2500%) scaleX(3) } to { transform: translateX(4900%) scaleX(1) } }
</style><style>/*---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *  Copyright (c) Microsoft Corporation. All rights reserved.
 *  Licensed under the MIT License. See License.txt in the project root for license information.
 *--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/

.mtks.mtku { text-decoration: underline line-through; text-underline-position: under; }</style><meta name="og:description" content="Leetcode 2. Add Two Numbers

You are given two **non-empty** linked lists, `l1` and `l2`, where each represents a non-negative integer.
    
The digits are stored in **reverse order**, e.g. the number 123 is represented as `3 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 1 -&gt;` in the linked list.

Each of the nodes contains a single digit. You may assume the two numbers do not contain any leading zero, except the number 0 itself.

Return the sum of the two numbers as a linked list.

**Example 1:**

![](https://imagedelivery.net/CLfkmk9Wzy8_9HRyug4EVA/fee72e19-6a21-45a5-365e-3cb45aba9700/public)

```java
Input: l1 = [1,2,3], l2 = [4,5,6]

Output: [5,7,9]

Explanation: 321 + 654 = 975.
```

**Example 2:**

```java
Input: l1 = [9], l2 = [9]

Output: [8,1]
```

**Constraints:**
* `1 &lt;= l1.length, l2.length &lt;= 100`.
* `0 &lt;= Node.val &lt;= 9`

&lt;br&gt;
&lt;br&gt;
&lt;details class=&quot;hint-accordion&quot;&gt;  
    &lt;summary&gt;Recommended Time &amp; Space Complexity&lt;/summary&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
    You should aim for a solution with &lt;code&gt;O(m + n)&lt;/code&gt; time and &lt;code&gt;O(1)&lt;/code&gt; space, where &lt;code&gt;m&lt;/code&gt; is the length of list &lt;code&gt;l1&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;n&lt;/code&gt; is the length of list &lt;code&gt;l2&lt;/code&gt;.
    &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;

&lt;br&gt;
&lt;details class=&quot;hint-accordion&quot;&gt;  
    &lt;summary&gt;Hint 1&lt;/summary&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
    Try to visualize the addition of two numbers. We know that the addition of two numbers is done by starting at the one's digit. We add the numbers by going through digit by digit. We track the extra value as a &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt; because the addition of two digits can result in a number with two digits. The &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt; is then added to the next digits, and so on. How do you implement this in case of linked lists?
    &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;

&lt;br&gt;
&lt;details class=&quot;hint-accordion&quot;&gt;  
    &lt;summary&gt;Hint 2&lt;/summary&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;
    We track the extra value, &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt;, here as well. We iterate through the lists &lt;code&gt;l1&lt;/code&gt; and &lt;code&gt;l2&lt;/code&gt; until both lists reach &lt;code&gt;null&lt;/code&gt;. We add the values of both nodes as well as the carry. If either of the nodes is &lt;code&gt;null&lt;/code&gt;, we add &lt;code&gt;0&lt;/code&gt; in its place and continue the process while tracking the carry simultaneously. Once we complete the process, if we are left with any &lt;code&gt;carry&lt;/code&gt;, we add an extra node with that carry value and return the head of the result list.
    &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;

</button><!----><!----><app-toast _ngcontent-mqa-c30="" _nghost-mqa-c26=""><div _ngcontent-mqa-c26="" class="notification is-light hidden is-danger"><fa-icon _ngcontent-mqa-c26="" class="ng-fa-icon icon"><svg role="img" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" data-prefix="fas" data-icon="exclamation-triangle" class="svg-inline--fa fa-exclamation-triangle fa-w-18" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path fill="currentColor" d="M569.517 440.013C587.975 472.007 564.806 512 527.94 512H48.054c-36.937 0-59.999-40.055-41.577-71.987L246.423 23.985c18.467-32.009 64.72-31.951 83.154 0l239.94 416.028zM288 354c-25.405 0-46 20.595-46 46s20.595 46 46 46 46-20.595 46-46-20.595-46-46-46zm-43.673-165.346l7.418 136c.347 6.364 5.609 11.346 11.982 11.346h48.546c6.373 0 11.635-4.982 11.982-11.346l7.418-136c.375-6.874-5.098-12.654-11.982-12.654h-63.383c-6.884 0-12.356 5.78-11.981 12.654z"></path></svg></fa-icon>  <button _ngcontent-mqa-c26="" class="delete"></button></div></app-toast></app-sign-in></div></div><app-sidebar _ngcontent-mqa-c60="" _nghost-mqa-c45=""><div _ngcontent-mqa-c45="" class="my-sidebar closed"><div _ngcontent-mqa-c45="" class="close-container cursor-hand"><button _ngcontent-mqa-c45="" class="button is-danger is-light" style="font-size: 12px;">ESC</button></div><!----></div><!----><!----><!----></app-sidebar></app-problem-navbar><!----><div _ngcontent-mqa-c63="" class="code-container problems-page"><div _ngcontent-mqa-c63="" class="code-block1" style="width: calc(45% - 8px);"><app-prompt _ngcontent-mqa-c63="" _nghost-mqa-c59=""><div _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="tabs is-left" style="width: 100%; overflow-x: hidden; margin-bottom: 0px;"><ul _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="tabs-list" style="width: 100%; margin-left: 0px;"><li _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="my-active-tab"><a _ngcontent-mqa-c59=""><span _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="tab-header bold-font">Question</span></a></li><li _ngcontent-mqa-c59=""><a _ngcontent-mqa-c59=""><span _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="tab-header light-text">Solution</span></a></li><li _ngcontent-mqa-c59=""><a _ngcontent-mqa-c59=""><span _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="tab-header light-text">Submissions</span></a></li><!----><li _ngcontent-mqa-c59=""><a _ngcontent-mqa-c59=""><span _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="tab-header light-text">Notes</span></a></li><!----></ul></div><div _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="question-tab" style="position: relative; padding-bottom: 50px; overflow-y: auto; height: 100%;"><div _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" style="padding: 24px;"><div _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="flex-container-row" style="justify-content: space-between; margin-bottom: 10px;"><h1 _ngcontent-mqa-c59="">Add Two Numbers</h1><!----></div><p _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" class="button is-rounded difficulty-btn is-warning" style="font-weight: bold; vertical-align: middle;">Medium</p><!----><app-article _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" fontsize="17px"><!----><div class="my-article-component-container"><div><p style="font-size: 17px;">You are given two <strong>non-empty</strong> linked lists, <code class="hljs language-undefined" style="font-size: 14.5px;">l1</code> and <code class="hljs language-undefined" style="font-size: 14.5px;">l2</code>, where each represents a non-negative integer.</p>
<p style="font-size: 17px;">The digits are stored in <strong>reverse order</strong>, e.g. the number 123 is represented as <code class="hljs language-basic" style="font-size: 14.5px;">3 -&gt; 2 -&gt; 1 -&gt;</code> in the linked list.</p>
<p style="font-size: 17px;">Each of the nodes contains a single digit. You may assume the two numbers do not contain any leading zero, except the number 0 itself.</p>
<p style="font-size: 17px;">Return the sum of the two numbers as a linked list.</p>
<p style="font-size: 17px;"><strong>Example 1:</strong></p>
<p style="font-size: 17px;"><img src="https://imagedelivery.net/CLfkmk9Wzy8_9HRyug4EVA/fee72e19-6a21-45a5-365e-3cb45aba9700/public" alt=""></p>
<div class="code-toolbar"><pre class="language-java" tabindex="0"><code class="hljs language-java" style="font-size: 14.5px;"><span class="token class-name" style="font-size: 14.5px;">Input</span><span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">:</span> l1 <span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">=</span> <span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">[</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">2</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">3</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">]</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span> l2 <span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">=</span> <span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">[</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">4</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">6</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">]</span>

<span class="token class-name" style="font-size: 14.5px;">Output</span><span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">:</span> <span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">[</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">5</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">7</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">9</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">]</span>

<span class="token class-name" style="font-size: 14.5px;">Explanation</span><span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">:</span> <span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">321</span> <span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">+</span> <span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">654</span> <span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">=</span> <span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">975.</span>
</code></pre><div class="toolbar"><div class="toolbar-item"><button class="copy-to-clipboard-button" type="button" data-copy-state="copy"><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<p style="font-size: 17px;"><strong>Example 2:</strong></p>
<div class="code-toolbar"><pre class="language-java" tabindex="0"><code class="hljs language-java" style="font-size: 14.5px;"><span class="token class-name" style="font-size: 14.5px;">Input</span><span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">:</span> l1 <span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">=</span> <span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">[</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">9</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">]</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span> l2 <span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">=</span> <span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">[</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">9</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">]</span>

<span class="token class-name" style="font-size: 14.5px;">Output</span><span class="token operator" style="font-size: 14.5px;">:</span> <span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">[</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">8</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">,</span><span class="token number" style="font-size: 14.5px;">1</span><span class="token punctuation" style="font-size: 14.5px;">]</span>
</code></pre><div class="toolbar"><div class="toolbar-item"><button class="copy-to-clipboard-button" type="button" data-copy-state="copy"><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<p style="font-size: 17px;"><strong>Constraints:</strong></p>
<ul style="font-size: 17px;">
<li><code class="hljs language-basic" style="font-size: 14.5px;">1 &lt;= l1.length, l2.length &lt;= 100</code>.</li>
<li><code class="hljs language-basic" style="font-size: 14.5px;">0 &lt;= Node.val &lt;= 9</code></li>
</ul>
<br>
<br>
<details class="hint-accordion">  
    <summary>Recommended Time &amp; Space Complexity</summary>
    <p style="font-size: 17px;">
    You should aim for a solution with <code class="hljs language-reasonml" style="font-size: 14.5px;">O(m + n)</code> time and <code class="hljs language-stylus" style="font-size: 14.5px;">O(1)</code> space, where <code class="hljs language-ebnf" style="font-size: 14.5px;">m</code> is the length of list <code class="hljs language-undefined" style="font-size: 14.5px;">l1</code> and <code class="hljs language-ebnf" style="font-size: 14.5px;">n</code> is the length of list <code class="hljs language-undefined" style="font-size: 14.5px;">l2</code>.
    </p>
</details>

<br>
<details class="hint-accordion">  
    <summary>Hint 1</summary>
    <p style="font-size: 17px;">
    Try to visualize the addition of two numbers. We know that the addition of two numbers is done by starting at the one's digit. We add the numbers by going through digit by digit. We track the extra value as a <code class="hljs language-ebnf" style="font-size: 14.5px;">carry</code> because the addition of two digits can result in a number with two digits. The <code class="hljs language-ebnf" style="font-size: 14.5px;">carry</code> is then added to the next digits, and so on. How do you implement this in case of linked lists?
    </p>
</details>

<br>
<details class="hint-accordion">  
    <summary>Hint 2</summary>
    <p style="font-size: 17px;">
    We track the extra value, <code class="hljs language-ebnf" style="font-size: 14.5px;">carry</code>, here as well. We iterate through the lists <code class="hljs language-undefined" style="font-size: 14.5px;">l1</code> and <code class="hljs language-undefined" style="font-size: 14.5px;">l2</code> until both lists reach <code class="hljs language-java" style="font-size: 14.5px;"><span class="token keyword" style="font-size: 14.5px;">null</span></code>. We add the values of both nodes as well as the carry. If either of the nodes is <code class="hljs language-java" style="font-size: 14.5px;"><span class="token keyword" style="font-size: 14.5px;">null</span></code>, we add <code class="hljs language-undefined" style="font-size: 14.5px;">0</code> in its place and continue the process while tracking the carry simultaneously. Once we complete the process, if we are left with any <code class="hljs language-ebnf" style="font-size: 14.5px;">carry</code>, we add an extra node with that carry value and return the head of the result list.
    </p>
</details></div></div><!----><!----></app-article><!----><div _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" style="font-size: 16px; padding-top: 50px;"></div><app-carbon _ngcontent-mqa-c59="" _nghost-mqa-c57=""><div _ngcontent-mqa-c57="" id="carbon-container"><script async="" id="_carbonads_js" type="text/javascript" src="//cdn.carbonads.com/carbon.js?serve=CW7IPKJN&amp;placement=neetcodeio&amp;format=cover"></script><div id="carbonads"><div id="carbon-responsive">
